2026-07-02T07:07:59.5559386Z   script: UPLOAD_DIR="/root/web01.1/apk-uploads"
BASE_URL="https://faxecez.eu.org"
find /tmp/cs_builds -maxdepth 1 -name "*.cs3" | while IFS= read -r new_file; do
  name=$(basename "$new_file")
  plugin_name="${name%.cs3}"
  old_file=$(find "$UPLOAD_DIR" -maxdepth 1 -name "*_${plugin_name}.cs3" 2>/dev/null | sort | tail -1)
  if [ -n "$old_file" ]; then
    cp "$new_file" "$old_file"
    echo "UPDATED: $plugin_name"
  else
    ts=$(date +%s%3N)
    dest="$UPLOAD_DIR/${ts}_${name}"
    cp "$new_file" "$dest"
    sz=$(stat -c%s "$dest")
    cd /root/web01.1 && node -e "try{const db=require('./database');db.addUploadedPlugin({internalName:'${plugin_name}',name:'${plugin_name}',description:'',authors:[],version:1,url:'${BASE_URL}/apk/${ts}_${name}',iconUrl:'',types:[],lang:'id',csStatus:1,filePath:'${dest}',fileSize:${sz:-0}});console.log('Registered: ${plugin_name}');}catch(e){console.error(e.message);}" 2>/dev/null || true
  fi
done
rm -rf /tmp/cs_builds
echo "Deploy complete"
